     vidyālabhyamuktau nātiśaya ityāha apica vidyāsādhanamiti /	vidyA laBya muktO na atiSayaH iti Aha  apica vidyA sADanam iti /
     nanu brahmaṇo nityasiddhatvādavidyānivṛtteścānyatve dvaitāpatteḥ,	nanu brahmaNaH nitya sidDa tvAt avidyA nivRtteH ca anya tve dvEta ApatteH,
     ananyatve cāsādhyatvādikaṃ vidyāphalamityata āha taddhīti /	ananya tve ca asADya tva Adikam vidyA Palam iti atas Aha tat Di iti /
     vidyayābhivyaktatvena brahmānanda eva	vidyayA aBivyakta tvena brahma AnandaH eva
     mukhyaphalamabhivyaktiravidyānivṛttirānandasvarūpasphūrtipratibandhakābhāvatayā	muKya Palam aBivyaktiH avidyA nivRttiH Ananda svarUpa sPUrti pratibanDaka aBAvatayA
     vidyayā sādhyate sā cānirvācyeti na dvaitāpattiḥ /	vidyayA sADyate sA ca anirvAcya iti na dvEtApattiH /
     anye tu sā brahmānanyetyāhuḥ /	anye tu sA brahmAn anyA iti AhuH /
     naca sādhyatvānupapattestatra vidyāvaiyarthyamiti vācyam /	na ca sADya tva anupapatteH tatra vidyA vEyarTyam iti vAcyam /
     yadabhāve yadabhāvastattatsādhyamiti jñānātsarvo lokaḥ pravartate /	yad aBAve yat aBAvaH tat tad sADyam iti jQAnAt sarvaH lokaH pravartate /
     yathāca vidyāyā abhāve brahmasvarūpamukterabhāvo 'nartharūpā	yaTA ca vidyAyAH aBAve brahma svarUpa mukteH aBAvaH anarTa rUpA
     avidyaivāsti /	avidyA eva asti /
     asyā avidyāyā eva muktirnāstītivyavahāraviṣayatvena muktyabhāvatvāt /	asyAH avidyAyAH eva muktiH na asti iti vyavahAra vizaya tvena mukti aBAva tvAt /
     tathāca vidyāṃ vinā muktirnāstīti niścayādvidyāmupādatte /	taTA ca vidyAm vinA muktiH na asti iti niScayAt vidyAm upAdatte /
     vidyodaye ca	vidyA udaye ca
     svataḥsiddhanityanivṛttānarthasvaprakāśabrahmānandātmanavatiṣṭhata	svatas sidDa nitya nivRtta anarTa sva prakASa brahma Ananda Atman avatizWata
     ityanavadyam /	iti anavadyam /
     saṃprati vidyāyāmatiśayāṅgīkāra tyajati naceti /	saMprati vidyAyAm atiSaya aFgIkAra tyajati nacA iti /
     ekarūpe viṣaye pramāyāṃ tāratamyānupapatterityarthaḥ /	eka rUpe vizaye pramAyAm tAratamya anupapatteH iti arTaH /
     kathaṃ tarhi pūrvādhikaraṇe vidyāyā viśeṣa uktaḥ, tatrāha tasmāditi /	kaTam tarhi pUrva aDikaraNe vidyAyAH viSezaH uktaH, tatra Aha tasmAt iti /
     satyāmapi sāmagryāṃ jñāne vilamba ukto na tāratamyamityarthaḥ /	satyAm api sAmagryAm jQAne vilambaH uktaH na tAratamyam iti arTaH /
     tarhi satyapi jñāne muktau vilambaḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha natviti /	tarhi sati api jQAne muktO vilambaH kim na syAt iti atas Aha natu iti /
     vāyvādipratibandhāddipotpattivilambe 'pyutpanne	vAyu Adi pratibanDAt dipa utpatti vilambe api utpanne
     tamonivṛttivilambādarśanātsati jñāne nājñānanivṛttau vilamba iti bhāvaḥ	tamaH nivRtti vilambA darSanAt sati jQAne na ajQAna nivRttO vilambaH iti BAvaH
     kiñca karmaṇāmupāsanānāṃ ca guṇabhedena tāratamyātphalatāratamyaṃ yuktam	kiQca karmaNAm upAsanAnAm ca guNa Bedena tAratamyAt Pala tAratamyam yuktam
     nirguṇavidyāyāstvekarūpatvāttatphalaikarūpyamityāha vidyābhedetyādinā /	nirguNa vidyAyAH tu eka rUpa tvAt tad Pala eka rUpyam iti Aha vidyA Beda ityAdinA /
     smṛtau kasyacinnirguṇavida ityarthaḥ /	smRtO kasyacid nirguNa vidaH iti arTaH /
     tasmādvidyāsamakālaiva muktiriti siddham //52//	tasmAt vidyA sama kAlA eva muktiH iti sidDam //52//

   śārīrakamīmāṃsābhāṣye tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ // 4 //	SArIrakamI mAMsa ABAzye tRtIya aDyAyasya caturTaH pAdaH // 4 //
     iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryaśrīgovindānandabhagavatkṛtau	iti SrImat paramahaMsa parivrAjaka AcArya SrI govinda Ananda Bagavat kRtO
     śārīrakavyākhyāyā bhāṣyaratnaprabhāṭīkāyāṃ tṛtīyasyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ	SArIraka vyAKyAyAH BAzya ratna praBAwIkAyAm tRtIyasya aDyAyasya caturTaH
